Full Text of the German Memorandum 18

(Berlin) The detailed content of the official reply issued by the German government on March 31 regarding the four-country draft proposal was announced by the authorities tonight. The main text of the reply is divided into two parts, in addition to the introduction and conclusion:

Part 1: Regarding the Rhineland issue and the signing of a non-aggression pact.

Part 2: Regarding concrete proposals for limiting armaments.

The main points of the entire reply are excerpted below:

Introduction: The German government, in order to complete genuine and effective international cooperation and to permanently maintain world peace, hereby drafts the entire text of this reply in accordance with the will of all German citizens and in accordance with the following two principles, and provides it for the reference of the governments and peoples of the countries concerned:

Principle 1: The freedom, independence, and equality of the German nation must absolutely maintain its integrity.

Principle 2: All future international conferences should be based on absolute equality, so that the honor of all participating countries is not harmed in the slightest.

(1) Explains the German government's views on the Rhineland issue since the signing of the Treaty of Versailles seventeen years ago, with excerpts from important speeches made by the German leader on this issue in the past three years.

(2) The German government is unwilling to submit disputes over its own territory to international courts. This is the duty of Germany to maintain its sovereign integrity.

(3) The German government believes that the difficult work currently facing European politicians can be completed in the following three stages:

A period of easing current tensions and preparing for future conference procedures.

A period of actual commencement of the conference.

A period of handling supplementary work on peacebuilding,

Such as disarmament and economic issues, etc.

(4) The German government hereby proposes the following peace plan based on the above three stages:

The international treaties to be signed in the future related to European peace should have a dignity that cannot be ignored by all countries. Therefore, at the time of signing, the governments of all countries should have an equal foothold of self-respect and respect for others.

The current state of anxiety should be eliminated as soon as possible. The German government intends to complete the signing of a broader "international non-aggression security pact" within four months.

If the governments of France and Belgium can guarantee the same spirit and action, Germany will never increase the military strength currently stationed in the Rhineland area or move German troops to areas closer to the borders of France and Belgium.

The German government proposes that England and Italy, as guarantor countries, form a temporary guarantee committee with another neutral country to guarantee the implementation of the above-mentioned promises.

The governments of Germany, France, and Belgium have the right to send representatives to participate in the above-mentioned guarantee committee. If any of the three countries, Germany, France, or Belgium, believes that its military position has changed, it also has the right to notify the committee.

Germany, France, and Belgium allow the military advisors of the two guarantor countries, Italy and England, to make reports based on the necessary investigations or inspections required by the above-mentioned notification.

If the guarantee committee has conflicting opinions, Germany, France, and Belgium are willing to accept and consider them as much as possible.

Germany is willing to accept all the requirements proposed by France and Belgium to restrict military activities on the Western Front, but only if these requirements are fully mutually complied with.

Germany, France, and Belgium agree to hold an open meeting with the two guarantor countries, England and Italy, under the leadership of the British government, immediately or as soon as possible after the French general election, to sign a security pact between Germany and France and Belgium, tentatively for a period of 25 years.

The German government agrees that England and Italy may sign this pact as guarantor countries.

Germany is extremely willing to fulfill its due obligations to sign all military mutual assistance subsidiary agreements arising from the above-mentioned security pact.

Germany reiterates the proposal to conclude a sky pact to supplement the shortcomings of the security pact.

The German government welcomes the participation of the Dutch government in the conclusion of the security pact.

France and Germany should do their best to eliminate all materials that may damage the friendship between the two countries in the education of young people and newspaper propaganda, so that the long-standing grievances between the two countries will be eliminated from now on.

The two countries agree to organize a joint committee to manage and investigate this task in order to achieve the above-mentioned goals.

Any pact signed by France and Germany should be approved by a general vote of the citizens of each country.

Germany is willing to have closer contact with its southeastern and eastern neighbors and invites them to participate in the security pact together.

Germany is willing to rejoin the League of Nations immediately or after the signing of the security pact.

Within a considerable period, Germany is willing to conduct friendly negotiations with the countries concerned to adjust colonial rights.

Germany suggests and hopes that the League of Nations covenant will be separated from the Treaty of Versailles as soon as possible.

Germany proposes the organization of an international arbitration court to monitor the implementation of the above-mentioned security pact and to review all disputes arising therefrom. The arbitration words have the power to bind all participating countries.

(1) The German government does not temporarily hope for the implementation of global disarmament or the implementation of a comprehensive arms reduction plan, believing that such efforts will be futile.

(2) All future disarmament conferences should have a clear and recognized goal in the sea, air, and land.

(3) The German government believes that restricting the scope of air force activities is very important and should be bound by the Geneva regulations regarding non-belligerent countries.

(4) The German government believes that the following matters should be decided by the disarmament conference as soon as possible:

Prohibit the use of poison gas bombs, asphyxiation bombs, and other ammunition containing toxic substances.

Towns and cities within the range of intermediate heavy artillery positions on the front lines should not be arbitrarily bombed by the air force.

Prohibit the bombardment of cities more than 20 kilometers away from the war zone with artillery fire.

Abolish heavy tanks.

Abolish heavy artillery.

(5) If all countries can comply with the obligations stipulated in the above five sections, the German government is willing to fulfill them without hesitation.

(6) The resolution of the disarmament issue is the prelude to the economic recovery movement, and the economic recovery movement is urgently needed for the construction of European peace. All countries should promote its early completion.

Conclusion: The German government's proposal of this entire proposal is a re-expression of efforts for the peace movement. It is believed that it has done its best to fulfill its duties. It is hoped that the people of other countries will no longer disappoint us, but will jointly help build world peace and economic recovery. (1st National Telegram)

Annual Meeting of the Mercantile Bank of London 20

(London) At today's meeting of the Mercantile Bank, Sir Mitchell spoke of China's abandonment of the silver standard, saying that we naturally cannot be without doubts about China's change to a managed currency system. The main reasons for the doubts can be summarized as follows: 1. The budget has not yet been balanced. 2. Customs duties and other government revenues are gradually decreasing. 3. The political situation in North China is very unstable. However, the stability of the current low exchange rate has encouraged the export of Chinese goods, and the trade balance has shown a more satisfactory trend in recent months than before. Mitchell also mentioned Japan, saying that Japan's recovery and commercial expansion since abandoning the gold standard continued unabated in 1935. He believed that the rise in cotton prices affected Japan more than Lancashire because the depreciation of the Japanese currency was even greater. However, the abundant supply of agile labor and lower living standards of Japanese industrialists may offset this adverse effect. Mitchell finally mentioned world trade, saying that there can only be hope of recovery if the administrations of various countries restore their soundness, and the artificial manipulation of agriculture and commerce becomes a more rational policy of allocating the production of goods according to the productive capacity of each country. However, looking at the current attitude of the world, I am afraid that this opportunity is still far away. (2nd Reuters Telegram)

Confirmed: Gonda, the Former Capital of Abyssinia, Falls 22

Stranglehold on the Road to Sudan; British Arms Supply Cut Off

Asmara: Gonda City, the capital of Amhara Province, 20 miles north of Lake Tsana, is an important town for the Abyssinian army on the northern route. It is stationed with more than 10,000 elite troops led by Abyssinian General Nasibu. It has now been occupied by Italian army light tank squadrons and armored vehicle squadrons. Italian military authorities here consider this the only achievement since the war, because Gonda City strangles the Abyssinian road to British Sudan. Most of the Abyssinian army's arms supply comes from the northern route. Now that the city has been occupied by the Italian army, the northern route has been cut off. (2nd National Telegram)

Front Line of Tigray Province, Abyssinia: According to our special correspondent Barr, the Madatha troops led by Italian Fascist Party Secretary General Starace occupied Gonda City, the former capital of Abyssinia, yesterday morning. These troops departed from Asmara City in Italian Eritrea and traveled 800 kilometers along the camel route (built in 1906) in 12 days to reach their destination. The Abyssinian troops defending the city did not resist and immediately retreated to the area 39 kilometers south of the city, near Lake Tsana. The residents of Gonda City are still safe and sound. (2nd Havas Telegram)

(Rome) The capture of Gonda City (on the northern route of Abyssinia), the former capital of Abyssinia, by the Italian army has a significant impact on the future situation of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, and its relationship with the European situation is also very important. After Italy's victory, it can participate more actively in European affairs. Not only that, the area near Gonda is a rich area in Abyssinia, and its occupation by the Italian army is also economically relevant. According to the fall of Gonda City, it had been expected more than ten days ago, and the Italian army entered the city without encountering any resistance. At this time, the Italian army and Lake Tsana, where the Blue Nile originates, are only dozens of kilometers apart. The water of the lake can be used to irrigate the cotton fields in British-Egyptian Sudan, which was originally the most important place for Britain. However, Prime Minister Mussolini has repeatedly stated that Italy has no intention of hindering the interests of other countries in Abyssinia, especially British interests. He would not break his word. (2nd Havas Telegram)

Frequent Conflicts on the Mongolian Border; Japan Prepares to Issue a Warning to Russia; Japanese Military Authorities Strongly Advocate Increasing Troops Stationed in Manchuria to Accomplish Continental Policies, Not Shrinking from Resorting to Force 24

(Nanjing) According to today's "National News," the Japanese government, regarding the frequent conflicts between "Manchukuo" and Outer Mongolia, will issue a final warning to Soviet Russia. Recent Conflict on the Mongolian Border 25

(Moscow) Kulun reports that the conflict between the Japanese-"Manchukuo" army and the Mongolian army at the Attik Dulun border guard outpost and Dammusik Bulak lasted throughout March 31 and part of April 1, ending on the morning of April 1.

On the morning of April 1, the Mongolian army repelled the repeated attempts of the Japanese-"Manchukuo" army to invade and occupy Dammusik Bulak, driving them back to the border, expelling them from Outer Mongolian territory, and inflicting heavy losses on them. The Attik Dulun outpost within Mongolian territory was reoccupied by Mongolian troops. (Second TASS dispatch)

(Moscow) Kulun reports that it has received a telegram from the commander of the Kwantung Army, describing the Japanese side's propaganda regarding the recent incident. According to the above report, the commander of the Kwantung Army, disregarding the fact that the Japanese army invaded Outer Mongolian territory dozens of kilometers and attempted to occupy Dammusik Bulak, falsely claimed that the incident was caused by the sudden invasion of Manchukuo territory by twelve Mongolian aircraft, which fiercely bombed the Japanese-"Manchukuo" troops. Therefore, the Japanese-"Manchukuo" troops had no choice but to counterattack the Mongolian aircraft. Kulun is extremely indignant at the commander of the Kwantung Army's shameless rumors, because he concealed the fact that the Japanese-"Manchukuo" army repeatedly attacked Dammusik Bulak (43 kilometers from the border) within Mongolian territory, attempting to occupy it, but was driven back to the other side of the border. Mongolian sources believe that the commander of the Kwantung Army intentionally misled public opinion, not only to the world, but also to Japan itself. (Second TASS dispatch)

Observations of British and American人士　Japan and Russia Will Not Go to War 26

Excessive propaganda by both sides startles the world　Unclear borders mean the powder keg will eventually explode

(London) The political situation is tense due to the frequent conflicts on the border between "Manchukuo" and Outer Mongolia, but all circles in London, both Japanese and Russian, remain calm and undisturbed. The newspapers here publish news about the Manchurian-Mongolian border disputes, but because the information is often unreliable, they do not comment on it. It is generally believed that the news transmitted by both sides is often exaggerated, mostly with the intention of startling the world. Today, a Reuters reporter interviewed a high-ranking official, who claimed that there is no clear border line between "Man" and Mongolia, because the terrain is flat and there are no landmarks to take. Therefore, it is almost impossible to demarcate the border line. The origin of the dispute is due to the fear of the Mongolian nomadic people of losing their grasslands. This is obviously incited by the propaganda of both Russia and Japan. Today's situation seems to be part of the overall strategy of both Russia and Japan. The frequent transmission of news of border disputes is largely aimed at arousing domestic public opinion, thereby opening up a way to comprehensively resolve the various outstanding issues between the two countries. It is difficult to believe that Japan or Soviet Russia intends to go to war. Both countries now have many important matters to deal with elsewhere, and they have no time to distract themselves. Therefore, if a war breaks out, they will inevitably lose everything and gain nothing. (First Reuters dispatch)

(New York) Howard, chairman of the Howard newspaper group, declared today after returning from a world tour that the unclear border between Outer Mongolia and Manchuria is most likely to cause the next world war. The location where the troops of both sides are currently fighting is actually the world's powder keg. It is reported that Howard's recent travels have taken him to the Far East, the Near East, and Europe, where he visited many international dignitaries and had a three-hour meeting with Stalin, Secretary General of the Soviet Russian Communist Party. Howard also said that the situation in Outer Mongolia seems slightly calmer than in Europe, but although the situation in Europe is very dangerous, a war may not break out within two years, because various countries are still brewing a new situation. British public opinion can be divided into two factions: one faction hopes that Britain will participate in a security organization to deter Germany, and the other faction advocates that Britain restore its former role as a peacemaker in order to maintain international balance and devote all its efforts to resisting the country with soaring arrogance. I feel that there are two hopes for a comprehensive solution in Europe now: Countries acknowledge that the Treaty of Versailles should be repealed; Accept discussions on restoring some of Germany's former colonies. Although this is not easy to achieve, Germany is prepared to accept it. Therefore, if Germany's desires are not too great, it will be a major factor in stabilizing the European situation and preventing war. (First National dispatch)

Hauptmann, the Lindbergh Kidnapping Case Offender, Lingers on His Last Breath 28

Trenton, New Jersey, USA: Warden Kimble of the State Prison yesterday ordered a stay of execution for Hauptmann. Today, he announced that the execution date has been changed to 8:00 PM on Friday. He further stated that if the court is still hearing the Wendel case at that time, he may issue another stay of execution. It is reported that the New Jersey Supreme Court ruled that the Hauptmann offender must be executed within one week starting from March 30. Therefore, Kimble may not be able to freely postpone the execution beyond Saturday. However, some observers say that the Hauptmann offender's fate is particularly good, and it may even be possible to extend his life until after the summer. The Mercer County Court will reconvene at 9:00 AM tomorrow to hear the Wendel case. Wendel is a dismissed military officer who is said to have initially admitted to participating in the Lindbergh baby kidnapping case, but later denied it. Therefore, if the jurors of the local court decide not to prosecute, then the Hauptmann offender will have no hope of survival. Otherwise, it may be possible to linger on his last breath for six months. (First National dispatch)

The Soviet Union Abolishes the Gold Ruble System; Paper Ruble Is Tied to the French Franc 29

(Moscow) Soviet Russia today officially abandoned the gold ruble and established a link between the paper ruble and the French gold franc. The exchange rate is set at one ruble for every three francs, and five rubles are equivalent to one US dollar. This change has no impact on the daily lives of the Soviet Russian people. However, foreigners who purchase daily necessities in Soviet Russia will pay four times the world price. (First National News Agency dispatch)

Our government has decided to request extradition in accordance with the ordinary criminal law of murder and is currently negotiating. As for the judges assigned to handle this case, because the trial was postponed and the original court's official duties were complicated, the two judges, Long Canya and Wu Shiheng, have returned to Jiangsu. National Cooperative Survey and Statistics 39

In addition, there were 332 preparatory cooperatives and mutual aid societies. Last year, the total amount of loans issued was 9,956,674 yuan, and the average circulating capital per member was 9.9 yuan. Last year, a total of 12,517 new cooperatives were added, with 486,290 members. There were also as many as 1,084 cooperatives that were dissolved. Furthermore, among the existing cooperatives in our country, classified by type, credit accounts for 59%, transportation and sales production each account for 9%, utilization accounts for 4%, purchasing accounts for 3%, and concurrent operations account for 16%. (Second Central News Agency dispatch)

Ancient Boat Discovered in Sui Ning 75

(Xuzhou) The Sui Ning Labor Service Corps supervised the people to excavate the city moat and unearthed a large boat on the side of the West Gate. It is about thirty feet long and eight feet wide, with four cabins. The boat planks are decayed, and there are many human bones and various artifacts inside. According to the Sui Ning County Records, Sui Ning was formerly the Sui River, which silted up to form the city, built in the Northern Song Dynasty. The sunken boat is located at the site of the old Sui River and should be an ancient boat over a thousand years old. (2nd, Central News Agency)

Record of the Public Trial of the Wang Case - Second Day of Trial of Li, Xiang, and Lu - Further Investigation of Evidence Required, Trial Adjourned 77

The case of the assassination of President Wang of the Executive Yuan was continued by the Fifth Branch of the Jiangsu High Court at 1:00 PM on the 31st at the Capital District Court's Criminal Court. The three defendants, Li Huaicheng, Xiang Zhonglin, and Lu Qingqi, were interrogated. The number of people attending the trial remained crowded, totaling four to five hundred. Central Committee members Chen Shuren, Wang Maogong, Gu Zhenggang, Gu Zhengding, etc., Executive Yuan Counselor Xu Xiangshu, etc., and representatives from various agencies also attended the hearing. The three defendants, Li, Xiang, and Lu, were extremely cunning and denied any knowledge of the details of the case. After the interrogation was completed, the defense lawyers expressed some opinions on the examination of evidence. The presiding judge stated that the case was serious and required further examination of the files and investigation of evidence. Therefore, he could not declare the conclusion of the debate on that day and announced that the court would reconvene on another day. All defendants were returned to custody. The following is a record of the interrogation of the three defendants, Li, Xiang, and Lu, on that day.

The records of confessions were read aloud, and the three defendants made slight corrections.

Shi Longcanya, Wu Yuheng, Prosecutor Luo Renji, Clerk Liu Jianze, etc., successively appeared in court. The defendants' defense lawyers Yu Zhongluo, Chen Liren, Liu Zhe, Chen Yaodong, Liu Liumin, Lin Dawen, Tao Rong, Bao YunGong, etc., also attended on time. The presiding judge then announced the opening of the court and continued the hearing of the case. First, the three defendants, Zhang Yuhua, He PoguAng, and Liu Shurong, were brought to court and instructed to first read the court records of the 30th. If there were any errors, they could be corrected. The clerk then read out the confessions of the defendants on the 30th one by one. Zhang made several corrections: As for yesterday’s testimony, the targets of the assassination were Chairman Jiang and President Wang. If neither could be achieved, they would fire a few random shots, but he did not say anything about disturbing public order. He PoguAng and Sun Fengming did not go to the Central Party Headquarters, this was not the case. He only obtained the entry and exit permit and gave it to Sun Fengming. The presiding judge said that it was not necessary to send it to the Central Party Headquarters, but rather just sending it to the gate or halfway there would be enough. The reason for the assassination was not dissatisfaction with Chairman Jiang and President Wang, but rather dissatisfaction with the general social situation and the increasingly chaotic state of affairs. He insisted that the record book of the Capital District Court had red lines, and was only quieted when the presiding judge showed him the record book with his signature. When writing the confession at the Gendarmerie Headquarters, the representative of the Central Committee said to me that if this was due to ideological errors, it could be explained, and there would be an opportunity for reflection, so I wrote it that way. I did not send Sun Fengming into the Central Party Headquarters, etc. Liu also made slight corrections. After each was recorded, they all signed the record book. The time was 2:08 PM.

Li's Cunning Attitude, Claiming Ignorance of Everything

The presiding judge then summoned Li Huaicheng. Li denied all points of the assassination conspiracy, claiming ignorance. His attitude was extremely cunning. According to what you confessed yesterday, you joined the Tongmenghui early on, and even in the 16th year of the Republic of China, you still held important positions in the Kuomintang and planned the revolution for the Premier. Given your efforts in the past, why did you join the reactionary organization this time and plot assassination? I didn’t join. I have been working for the revolution for decades, and my purpose has never changed. You were the principal of Zhongying Middle School, weren’t you? That was founded by me. When did you know that He PoguAng, Zhang Yuhua, Hua Kezhi, etc., had organized the Chenguang News Agency? A little over a month before the incident. How did you know about the Chenguang Agency? Because my friend Xiang Zhonglin lived there, that's how I knew. Do you often go to the Chenguang Agency? Not often. Because I have rheumatism, I go to the Xinjiekou Hospital for treatment and then conveniently visit him. When my illness is better, I also invite him to play at Houhu. I go there with no purpose. Do you know the purpose of their organizing the Chenguang Agency? I don’t know. When did you know that the Chenguang Agency was a cover for assassination? Only after the incident did I know. Do you know who is in charge of the Chenguang Agency? I only know that the person in charge is He ShaoRu. He is the president. I didn’t even know his name was He PoguAng. Do you know Hua Kezhi (that is, Hu Yunqing)? I don’t know. Who took you to the Chenguang Agency? Xiang Zhonglin. He lived there for a long time. After I met him, he took me there, but whether he took me there, I am now unsure. Are Xiang Zhonglin and you good friends? Very good. Did Xiang Zhonglin know that the Chenguang Agency was an assassination organization? Did he tell you? I don’t know if he knew, but he didn’t tell me. I only know that this organization was registered and supervised by the government. Did you ask Xiang Zhonglin what he came to Nanjing for? He said he was trying to get a tobacco and alcohol license for Ma Renqi (transliteration). Do you know Zhang Yuhua? I don’t know. I only know his name is Zhang Siming.

Denies Home is Communication Hub

But that’s not the truth. Xiang Zhonglin confessed at the Gendarmerie Headquarters that the assassination organization used your home as a communication hub. Since Xiang Zhonglin is your good friend, he certainly wouldn’t try to implicate you. I don’t know about that. If he confessed that way, he’s just trying to frame me. That’s simply ridiculous. On October 28th, there was a discussion meeting to discuss the assassination. Were you there? I was there. I didn’t go that day because I had something to do. I originally asked Xiang Zhonglin to go to Shanghai, but he said that the entry and exit permit for the Central Party Headquarters had not yet been obtained and he couldn’t go with me. Soon, it was time for dinner. I even drank a little sorghum wine and got a little drunk. After finishing dinner, I went to the next room. Xiang Zhonglin leaned on the bed, and I also sat on the bed. I talked to Xiang about Buddhism. I not only believe in it, but I also have a deep and unified spirit. As for Liu Shurong, Zhang Yuhua, He PoguAng, Sun Fengming, Hua Kezhi, etc., I don't know how they came in. They were talking messily. I didn’t pay attention. I only heard them talking about movies, Buddhism, and international issues. Later, they talked about the Chinese situation. Hua Kezhi made some comments. Later, they talked about Chairman Jiang. Everyone was dissatisfied with Chairman Jiang, and I strongly disagreed. I said that they didn’t have a clear understanding of people or the situation. Later, Sun Fengming, out of character, said some very radical and illegal things. What illegal things did Sun say? He said he wanted to assassinate. What did you say? I said that such things are not easy to talk about. It’s better to do less. At that time, my head was dizzy. I think I said these things. Then I went back.

Very Confused During the Conversation

Didn't you say that doing this kind of thing requires determination, otherwise, don't take on the task, and success will be heroic? I was very confused. The presiding judge rebuked him, saying that now that you have become a defendant, your mind is confused. Were you also confused at that time? During the meeting, was President Wang mentioned? That wasn’t a meeting. President Wang was not mentioned at all. What did they want to use to assassinate? Do you know? I don’t know. Have you seen this gun? No. Xiang Zhonglin told you that the entry and exit permit from the Central Party Headquarters would be used for something. Did he? He said he was exchanging it for a new entry and exit permit. Exchanging the entry and exit permit is a very common thing. Why did he talk to you about it? I asked him if he was going back to Shanghai. That’s how it came up. Did you ask him why he needed to exchange it? No. When they wanted to assassinate, why didn't you stop them? You must have agreed to it too. I was dizzy and didn’t bother to speak that day. On the 30th, you saw Sun Fengming again. Did he say anything to you? I saw that his attitude was different from usual. He was very peaceful, very excited, and very polite. He poured me a cup of tea. I said to him that your point of view is wrong. You said you saw his attitude was different from usual, right? I said he was at peace.

Advised Him Not to Assassinate Chairman Jiang

What exactly did you say to him? I advised him. I said, their observation point is wrong. I also explained for Chairman Jiang (at that time, I called him Mr. Jiang), saying that they recognized the wrong person and the wrong situation. I said that Mr. Jiang is very important. Whoever harms Chairman Jiang will bear the responsibility for the destruction of the country and the extermination of the race. They will become traitors. He showed me great sincerity and called me Old Huai, believing that my words were correct, and then sent me out. Why did you go this time? I went to see Xiang Zhonglin. When I went, he had already moved out. I don't know why he moved out. Why did you suddenly ask Sun Fengming about Chairman Jiang? Because of what happened on the evening of the 28th. I was not encouraging him. Because young people often do this kind of thing, it was just a general discussion.

Denies Advocating the Assassination of Wang

On the afternoon of November 15th last year, at 4:00 PM, you confessed at the Gendarmerie Headquarters that they had decided to assassinate Chairman Jiang. You said that assassinating Chairman Jiang is not as good as assassinating President Wang, because assassinating President Wang brings glory, and death is also glorious. You told Sun Fengming to hurry up and do it. You said that you changed their plan. Why don’t you confess today? This is a rumor! (The whole audience laughed) This is not my confession. These were my conversations with another defendant surnamed Wang in the Gendarmerie Headquarters. If it was a conversation between you and another defendant, how could the Gendarmerie Headquarters record it? I don’t know. You confessed that you were an anarchist, right? I said that I am an anarchist with the unity of mind and matter. This is my explanation of the unity of mind and matter in Buddhist scriptures. You also confessed that He PoguAng was responsible for the practical affairs of the agency, Hua Kezhi was responsible for the finances, and Wang Yaqiao directed the assassination of Wang, right? This is really inexplicable! Whether these words are mine or not is still a question. As for the background of the Chenguang Agency, I only found out later. When I got to Shanghai, they told me to avoid it. Only then did I know the background of the Chenguang Agency. The prosecutor of this court asked you about setting up a communication hub in your home, and you admitted it. I don’t know how they sent letters. I wasn’t at home. After the incident, He PoguAng found a telegram for Zhang Yuhua, which was forwarded from your home, right? I don’t know. Zhang Yuhua’s confession explains this very clearly. How could I know? My family has a wife, children, and elders, and we have lived there for more than ten years. How could it be a communication hub? You have a son. What’s his name? His name is Zhongying (transliteration).

Son Confessed to Receiving Subsidies

He was also involved in the case. He confessed that he had seen Hua Kezhi and He PoguAng, but not Zhang Yuhua. Hua Kezhi had seen me at home four or five times. He did not know about the assassination of President Wang. Usually, the letters were forwarded from my home, and they came to pick them up themselves. Hua Kezhi often gave our family ten or twenty yuan at a time. Your son confessed all of this. Why are you denying it? I have also helped Hua Kezhi before. When I wasn’t home, it was normal for the family to borrow ten or twenty yuan from him. But I don’t know about this matter. I didn’t ask them to forward letters at my home. Then why did they have to forward them from your home? I only know that Mo Xiong, Zhang Ziyu, etc., have forwarded letters at my home. They are all people from the Central Committee. But your son’s confession said that the letters of He PoguAng and Zhang Yuhua were also forwarded from your home. He PoguAng and I have no relationship at all. Have you been to Fujian? I have. I went with Hua Kezhi and Xiang Zhonglin. What did you do there? Because Xiang’s wife taught in Fujian, and the principal of that school is also my friend, so I went to see them. Did you work in the People's Government? No. When we arrived in Fujian, the flag of the People’s Government was just raised. I have never met anyone from the People’s Government. Do you know Wang Yaqiao? I know him. He also knew the Premier. When did you come to Nanjing? Last August or September. Zhang Yuhua confessed that the money for the Chenguang Agency was provided by Wang Yaqiao, who received it from Chen Mingshu and Li Jishen. Do you know that? I don’t know. When I was in Shanghai, Guo Weizhong told me to hide. Only then did I know the content. If you have nothing to do with the Chenguang Agency, why do you need to hide? Because of the dinner that day. But I have nothing to fear and did not hide. Eating a dinner is not a big deal. Why do you need to hide? Because they said some radical things.

Not Responsible for This Case at All

According to what you said, you have no relationship with the case. Why don’t you tell us yourself what responsibilities do you hold? I bear no responsibility at all. At this point, the presiding judge thought that although Li was extremely cunning, the facts were all there, and he could not avoid them. Then, he summoned Xiang Zhonglin. However, Chen Yaodong, the lawyer defending Li, stood up and said that whether or not a communication hub was set up in the defendant Li Huaicheng’s home was very important. This matter can be found in Zhang Yuhua’s confession, but Zhang denied the confession. He requested that the court question Zhang Yuhua on this point immediately. The presiding judge then asked Zhang Yuhua, but Zhang denied the communication hub issue, only saying that he sometimes forwarded letters from there. The presiding judge asked about the content of the letters. Zhang said that they were ordinary letters.

Xiang Was Once a Kidnapper, Lived in Three Cunning Lairs in Shanghai

At 3:15 PM, Xiang Zhonglin was summoned for questioning. When did you arrive at the Chenguang Agency? Last year. Why? Zhang Yuhua wanted me to get subsidies, so I lived there since everyone in the agency were scholars. Did you raise subsidies? No. Do you know the nature of Chenguang Agency? I saw He PoguAng and Liu Shurong visit the news during the day and issue the manuscript at night. It was a news agency. But the Chenguang Agency is an assassination cover, everyone knows it. I only knew after seeing the newspaper. Didn’t they explain it when they called you to go? No. How long did you live in Chenguang Agency? A few months, during which I went to Zhenjiang a few times. You lived for a few months, and you still don't know their secrets? I do not know. When did you meet He PoguAng? I met them at the Fuzhou Hotel. When did you meet Zhang Yuhua? I knew them before. You really didn't know that Chenguang Agency was an assassination agency? I do not know. Did you get the entry and exit permit from the Central Party Headquarters? I did not get it. He PoguAng asked me to say a word. I didn't know it was for Sun Fengming. You don't know what the entry and exit permit is used for? I do not know. You confessed at the Gendarmerie Headquarters that Sun Fengming came to the agency and asked me to get the entry and exit permit, so I knew they were going to assassinate, didn't you? I didn't make this confession. You confessed before that the secret communication agency was set up in Li Huaicheng's home, didn't you? Ordinary letters were transferred in his house. I didn't say it was a secret agency. How much money did you put in Chenguang Agency? Dozens of dollars. This is a friend to friend. How was the entry and exit permit obtained? I introduced He PoguAng to Xu Renru. I do not know who got it. You have a friend, why call He PoguAng to go? Because the department is different. (To be continued)

Serious Disaster in Northern Xu: More Than 800,000 Victims, Food Depleted, Urgent Relief Needed 78

A telegram from Xuzhou reports that in the areas of Tongshan, Pi, Pei, and Feng, since the Yellow River flood disaster, the number of victims has reached 800,000. Last winter, the provincial disaster relief association and various charities provided winter relief, but it was like a drop in the bucket, with little effect. This spring, after the ice melted, there were repeated strong winds, causing the land that had dried out and been sown by farmers to be flooded again. The victims, having lost all hope for the spring harvest, are increasingly desperate for food. Furthermore, from Fengbei in the west to Pinan in the east, along a route of hundreds of miles, the area remains a vast expanse of water. The victims have almost completely run out of food. As for the types of food, one is digging for sweet potatoes. Last year, when the Yellow River surged, the sweet potatoes that had barely formed were submerged in the water. Now that the land has dried out, the sweet potatoes have been soaked and rotted over the winter. Lacking food, the victims dig them up to eat. Another is pulling up wheat seedlings. In the land that was not flooded, wheat was sown last winter. This spring, the wheat seedlings have sprouted to a height of just over an inch. At night, the victims go to the fields and pull them up to eat, like cattle and horses. Another is peeling tree bark. Elm bark can be used as food, so the victims are out everywhere peeling it. However, they are suffering from the fact that the leaves have not grown and the bark is limited. Even this small amount is often fought over, a sight that should bring tears to one's eyes. As for where people are living, they are on high ground near the water, in villages under the trees, with grass shacks everywhere. They huddle inside, dressed in rags. There are men and women who exchange clothes to go out and search for food. Those with young children and weak daughters carry them in baskets to sell them in wealthier villages to be servants or concubines. Parents and children are separated in tragic farewells. Some even commit suicide by drowning to end their miserable lives. Those who are fortunate enough to be taken in as child brides or concubines are already living as if in heaven. Meanwhile, the wealthy households in the villages, fearing the difficulty of getting through the spring famine, are hoarding grain and not selling it, causing grain prices to rise daily. The only flour company in Xubu, which previously went to Shaanxi to purchase wheat under the guise of disaster relief, intending to sell third-grade flour at a fair price, has also recently seen its prices soar. The entire society is experiencing economic panic, and the victims are suffering even more. The cities and villages that were not affected by the disaster last year exhausted their efforts and resources in building the west dike of Micro Lake, levying labor and taxes. At present, they can only rely on foreign capital to provide spring relief.

The Tongshan District Commissioner's Office originally planned to organize a spring work relief program in Northern Xu to: Reconstruct the west dike of Micro Lake; Establish the Linjiaba sluice gate; Dredge the Bulao River. However, the provincial government only allocated 150,000 yuan, which is not even enough to reconstruct the dike. According to instructions, the District Commissioner's Office first sent Zhou Yushan, a resident engineer in Xu, to form a survey team. The Construction Bureau also sent Yu Shufang to Xu to provide guidance. They are immediately conscripting strong laborers from the disaster area for the work. The Provincial General Relief Association, at the invitation of the District Commissioner's Office, sent Wang Xiaobai, Chen Huichen, and Qiu Xiang as the heads of disaster relief investigation for the four counties of Tongshan, Pi, Pei, and Feng, arriving in Xu to set off. The District Commissioner's Office also appointed disaster relief investigators to assist them. However, the scope of the work relief is too small, only reconstructing the dike and not dredging the river, which is a great concern to all sectors of society. A joint meeting was held the other day, arguing that last year the provincial government, in order to ensure the Huai River diversion project, left Xu and Hai in a state of ruin. The four counties of Xu, with their meager remaining strength, fought the Yellow River for several months, ultimately bearing the brunt of the disaster to protect the Jiang and Huai regions. Therefore, if large-scale work relief is not carried out in the Xu region to clear the waterways, the suffering will never end. They specially jointly requested the District Commissioner's Office to strongly advocate for work relief, so as to achieve the goal of thoroughly dredging the river, in order to give the victims respite. It is unknown whether approval will be granted. The Chinese-American Relief Association has also allocated funds to build roads as a form of work relief. Construction has already begun, but the funds are only 4,000 yuan, which is also too little. The Xubu Red Swastika Society has recently set up a porridge factory to help the poor. It is also providing small-scale relief to the victims. Every day, people bringing children and daughters to the society's door to receive relief is a sight that one cannot bear to witness. (April 1st)

Guangdong Province Plans to Levy a Special Tax on Imported Luxury Goods, Due to Significant Deficit in Foreign Trade, Aiming to Reduce the Difference by Implementing a Special Tax 79

A telegram from Guangzhou reports that although Guangdong Province has recently increased the special tax on agricultural products, and various factories in the interior have also been established one after another, with local goods being produced in a steady stream, due to social habits, there is still a strong tendency to purchase imported goods. Moreover, due to its proximity to the ocean, smuggled and untaxed foreign goods are easily imported. Therefore, according to monthly statistics, foreign trade is still in a state of trade deficit. According to the investigation, in the three months of October, November, and December last year, the total value of imported foreign goods in the province was 37,155,475 yuan, while the total value of exported local goods was 19,889,783 yuan. Comparing the two, the trade deficit in the last three months of last year reached 17,265,692 yuan. In January of this year (25th year of the Republic), the total value of imported foreign goods was 8,004,449 yuan, while the total value of exported local goods was 6,399,143 yuan. The trade deficit for that month was 1,605,306 yuan. Comparing this to January of last year (24th year of the Republic), when the total value of imported foreign goods was 11,491,845 yuan and the total value of exported local goods was 7,634,453 yuan, the import of foreign goods in January of this year has decreased the trade deficit by 3,487,396 yuan. Although the trade deficit seems to have decreased slightly, it has not yet escaped the trade deficit status, and the deficit remains unaddressed. Recently, members of the Political Research Association specially proposed implementing a special tax on imported luxury goods to prevent the large-scale import of foreign goods and to reduce the deficit. The original proposal roughly stated, "According to investigation, the import of foreign luxury goods in this province is very large. In the 21st year of the Republic, the import value was over 5.06 million yuan, in the 22nd year it was over 5.65 million yuan, and in the 23rd year it was over 7.02 million yuan, averaging over 5.91 million yuan per year. The rate of increase in imports is also very high. Comparing the three years, the 22nd year increased by 12% compared to the 21st year, and the 23rd year further increased to 39%. Considering that our country's economy is backward and production is declining, the consumption of luxury goods beyond the necessities of life should be gradually reduced, but it is increasing year by year, which is completely contrary to the modern principles of advocating frugal consumption and using national capital to develop production. Moreover, this province's foreign trade has a long-term trade deficit. In the past ten years, the average annual trade deficit has reached 106 million yuan, with capital flowing out continuously. If this continues, it will inevitably lead to financial exhaustion, and the national economy and people's livelihood will be in a dangerous state. Furthermore, since the implementation of currency management policies, foreign trade has become even more important. If we do not prevent the import of non-essential items, how can we reduce the adverse trend of the trade gap and stop the deficit? Based on the above, the implementation of a special tax on imported luxury goods is urgently needed. According to the investigation, apart from wireless radio equipment, phonograph equipment, automobile equipment, and photographic materials that cannot be self-made, other luxury imports, such as perfumes, cosmetics, ornaments, etc., can all be self-made. Although they may not be as exquisite as foreign products, from the perspective of customs tariff protection policy to protect infant industries, a special tax should be increased to strengthen the competitiveness of domestic goods. Furthermore, from the perspective of social policy, luxury goods are mostly used by the wealthy. Increasing the special tax is also not too harsh, as it is taking from the rich without being oppressive, and it does not violate the principle of tax fairness. During the previous European war, Germany, France, Italy, and the United States all heavily taxed imported luxury goods, and modern countries all heavily tax luxury goods, because it is beneficial to the national economy without any harm. If this province levies this special tax, it is estimated that it can increase the treasury revenue by several million yuan each year, which can be used to supplement the treasury funds during this time of financial crisis. However, there are many types of imported luxury goods. Apart from those that are already taxed (such as seafood products like abalone, sea cucumber, and shark fin, which are already subject to a seafood tax; coffee, cocoa, raisins, and fruit juice, which are already subject to a agricultural special tax; beer, brandy, and whiskey, which are already subject to a liquor tax; and silk yarn, tobacco leaves, and cigars, which are already subject to tobacco and alcohol tax or consolidated tax; and fabrics such as wool, silk satin, rayon etc. which are already subject to foreign fabric tax.) Those that are not yet taxed, specially propose to formulate tax rates according to their quality, price, and needs, and list them in the following table. Whether it is appropriate is still subject to public decision." According to the investigation, this case was proposed for discussion on the 25th. The proposed tax rate for imported luxury goods is to levy a tax of 70% to 80% of the value. The categories of luxury goods mainly belong to cosmetics, jewelry, ornaments, smoking accessories, perfumes, foreign soaps, games, children's toys, etc. (March 27th)

Jiading: Three Arsonists Apprehended 80

The homes of Liao Shigong, Shiyun, and Shiyuan on Xueqiao North, Sicheng South Street, were set on fire three times in the past year, in October of the previous year and on February 4th and 8th of this year. Fortunately, the fires were extinguished, and only one firewood shed and half of a bedroom were burned. No major disaster occurred. Now, the Public Security Bureau has apprehended Zhou Shiming, Liang Yuezhou, and Wang Fuda, all of whom are members of the Seven Star Party. According to Zhou's confession, he is the brother-in-law of Zhao Ruisheng, a tenant of the Liao family. He held a grudge after failing to borrow money from Liao, and he does not deny committing arson. The Public Security Bureau believes the case is serious and is continuing to investigate. Once all the suspects have been apprehended, they will be handed over to the county court for handling.

Changshu: Fabric Industry to Suspend Operations 81

The weaving factories, the only major side occupation in the rural areas here, mostly ship their products to Shanghai for distribution to various places. Now, they have been abolished by the consolidated tax, which has led to a standstill in the sales and shipping problem. All the products of the factories are piling up. It is estimated that there are more than 80 weaving factories, large and small, and they ship about 6,000 bolts of fabric per day. At about three yuan per bolt, the daily value of goods being held up is 18,000 yuan. This has been going on for three days. Merchants do not have such a large amount of funds to circulate. If the hold-up reaches a week, the source of income for the weaving factories will be cut off, and they will inevitably have to suspend operations entirely. The reason for this is that, according to the established practice of shipping fabric, when shipping out, it is necessary to fill out a shipping form at the Changshu Inspection Office of the Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui Consolidated Tax Bureau before loading. Now, the inspection office was suddenly ordered to be abolished at the end of the month. No clear instructions have been given on how to handle the shipping of factory fabric. Therefore, all the products of the factories are piling up. If a solution is not found urgently, once the fabric factories suspend operations, the livelihoods of the tens of thousands of workers will also be affected. The Fabric Factory Association has decided to send Wu Hongfan and Wang Guanqin by train to Shanghai on the morning of the 2nd to join the Shanghai representatives in petitioning the Consolidated Tax Bureau for a solution.

Suzhou: Tangjiawan in Luzhi Robbed by Bandits 82

Tangjiawan, five li from Luzhi Town, was suddenly attacked by four bandit boats carrying thirty to forty bandits at one o'clock in the morning on one day. The bandits landed and robbed the home of Jin Hui Gao. The villagers beat gongs and gathered to resist, fighting hand-to-hand for an hour. Due to a lack of weapons, they were eventually defeated, and the bandits escaped with their loot. Jin Zi Ah Huo, 25 years old, was shot three times in the waist by the bandits and died on the spot. The injured villagers included Jin Bugao, Lu Nianchun, Tao Chuntang, Jiang Xiaogen, and Jin Aisheng, who were all shot in the waist, shoulders, and other places. The local headman, Yan Pingao, came to the city to report the incident to the local court on the afternoon of (the 2nd). The local court will send officials to the village for an on-site investigation today (the 3rd).

Nantong: Son-in-Law Strangles Father-in-Law 83

Zhai Changgui, who worked as a clerk in the Niuqiaozi area of Sian, gambled with his son-in-law, Sun Xifei, in the Wu Surname Dyeing Workshop. That night, he was strangled to death in the swamp by Sun and his gambling friends. After the case was discovered, Sun Xifei was arrested by the court. During an interrogation on the first day, he vehemently denied it. Because the accomplices are still at large, he has been detained pending further investigation.

Haizhou: Residents Near Yuntai Mountain Starve 84

The villages of Jinwan, Shandong, Gecun, Donglei, and those near Yuntai Mountain in Lianyungang City, have been severely affected by the crop failure last year and the Yellow River floods. Many are almost empty. As the days grow longer during this spring famine, the livelihoods of the residents are becoming increasingly precarious. Selling utensils and clothing and digging for wild grass roots can be seen everywhere. According to surveys, the number of households without a single meal per day has reached more than 200. There have also been instances of people committing suicide due to starvation.

Food Exports Cause Panic Among the Poor 85

Since the Yellow River floods last year, the autumn harvest was swept away by the floods, and no winter wheat was planted. Since the beginning of spring, there has been a significant shortage of food for the people. Recently, unscrupulous merchants in Xinpu, for the sake of profit, have been buying up large quantities of food and shipping them to Tianjin, Qingdao, Yantai, Dalian, and other places by train and ship, totaling no less than ten thousand piculs per day. As a result, the prices of all kinds of food have been soaring. At this time of the "hungry gap" between seasons, allowing food to be exported is causing widespread panic among the poor.

Yangzhou: Scenic Area Association to Expand Membership 86

The Management Committee of the Scenic Area North of the City held a meeting at the Education Bureau at 3:00 PM on the first day, resolving to expand the number of committee members and establish a Guidance Section. The county government sent letters to Wang Maoru, Ye Xiufeng, Yu Jingtang, Zhao Dihua, Hong Lanyou, Tang Yuzhong, Chen Hefu, Xu Xinwu, Zhou Shaowei, Hu Bijiang, and sixteen others to serve as members of the Guidance Section. Ling Shaozu, Bao Mingshu, Zhang Guoren, Jiang Taihua, and Zhou Xiangting were appointed as members of the Editorial Section.

Yangqing Buses to Run Directly Starting Today 87

The Yangqing Road long-distance buses, originally running from Shaobo to Qingjiang, were shortened to run from Shaobo to Gaoyou due to the reconstruction of bridges in the Gaoyou area. Now that the bridge has been completed, the Highway Administration has decided to restore the original route from Shaobo directly to Qingjiang, starting on the first day, for the convenience of travelers.

Central Savings Branch Opens 88

On that day, many representatives from various organizations and local dignitaries came to offer congratulations. Ningbo: Robbery Occurs in Yaojiapu, Yindong 89

Yao Zuoda, a resident of Yaojiapu in Yindong, is wealthy and honest, making him a long-time target for bandits. Around midnight on the other day, several bandits suddenly came, armed with weapons, and climbed over the wall into the house. They ransacked the house, searching through boxes and cabinets at will for about an hour before leaving fully loaded. It is estimated that gold, silver, clothing, and ornaments worth no less than several thousand yuan were stolen.

Bengbu: Public Memorial Service for Martyrs of the Seventeenth Army 90

The public cemetery for the soldiers of the Seventeenth Army who died in battle is located on the sunny side of Bengshan Mountain. It is the burial site for the martyrs of Xu Tingyao's troops who died in the suppression of the Red Army and the resistance against Japan. The cemetery is built against the mountain, with a magnificent structure, completed on April 1, 1934. Pavilions and terraces are hidden among the flowers and trees, creating a landscape with a park-like atmosphere, one of the most famous landmarks here. Now, the Public Cemetery Management Committee, in order to commemorate the merits of the martyrs and promote the national spirit, held a ceremony at 10:00 AM on the first day to commemorate the second anniversary of the cemetery's completion. Xu Tingyao, being in Beijing, was unable to come, so he specially sent Kai Jiao Mei, the former chief of staff of the Seventeenth Army, to Bengbu as his representative to participate in the public memorial service. About 200 people from all walks of life participated at that time. The meeting was solemn and respectful, with the memorial service conducted according to regulations. Kai Jiao Mei gave a detailed report on the Seventeenth Army's campaign to suppress the Red Army in western Anhui and the resistance against Japan at Gubeikou. Representatives from all sectors of society gave speeches one after another, all expressing their admiration for the martyrs and encouraging their colleagues to work together to overcome national difficulties and save the country. The ceremony ended at 12:00 PM.

The Taxpayer's Association Requests the Shanghai Municipal Council to Protect Patriotic Movements and Not Hinder the Collection of Aviation Donations from Hotels and Other Businesses 96

The Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the International Settlement sent a letter yesterday to the Secretary-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council, stating: "Regarding the letter from the Shanghai Hotel Industry Association, dated March 18th, reporting that members of the Public Concession, including the Oriental, Da Zhonghua, Jue Lu, Shenzhou, Central, New World, and New Huizhong hotels, stated that the Shanghai Municipal Council Patrol Force recently dispatched several detectives to force them to hand over all their aviation salvation fund triplicate receipt books for review. They also threatened to impose fines or revoke business licenses if they continued to collect donations, unreasonably forcing them to stop collecting without any room for argument. We request a reasoned and forceful appeal on the matter."

"It has been determined that the collection of aviation salvation funds is a national patriotic movement and a duty that should be fulfilled by citizens. The Municipal Council's interference is completely unfounded. Our association believes that this is not only a matter of stopping the collection of aviation salvation funds in one industry, but it is also hindering the entire aviation salvation movement and is a serious illegal event. We request that your council immediately lodge a strong protest with the Municipal Council to ensure that the same situation does not occur again, in order to benefit the patriotic movement."

"Also, the Shanghai Restaurant Industry Aviation Salvation Donation Committee sent a letter stating: 'Our committee convened fellow restaurateurs and organized the Shanghai Restaurant Industry Aviation Salvation Donation Committee. With the patriotic enthusiasm of the people, we voluntarily raised aviation salvation funds to assist the government and promote aviation. We have already submitted a request to the Chinese Aviation Association, which was forwarded to the Shanghai Municipal Government for approval. Since the start of the collection, the results have been quite good. Unexpectedly, the Concession authorities have been obstructing us in every possible way, and recently they have intensified their efforts, sending detectives to warn various restaurants not to collect donations, otherwise they would revoke their business licenses. They also tore down municipal government announcements and forcibly collected triplicate receipts. The actions of the Concession authorities clearly show that they are deliberately obstructing our people's patriotic movement. If we do not seriously negotiate, the nation's prestige will be lost, and the position of our compatriots in the Concession will also lose its guarantee. Under this oppression, the members of our committee are filled with indignation. We hereby request your association to negotiate with all your strength as soon as possible to facilitate the progress.'"

"The Executive Committee of this association discussed the proposal and unanimously agreed that 'the aviation salvation donation arising from the patriotic movement has been legally permitted, and no individual or group has the right to interfere or obstruct it, regardless of whether the interference or obstruction is out of good or bad intentions. The patriotic movements of foreigners in the Public Concession have never been interfered with or obstructed. This may prove that the actions of the patrol force were not taken under orders.'"

"It was immediately resolved that 'the Shanghai Municipal Council should be severely restrained and guarantee that the same incidents will not occur again and that legal protection should be provided.'"

"Accordingly, we hereby request your council to strictly order restraint and guarantee that the same incidents will not occur again and to provide legal protection to avoid causing misunderstandings and complicating the situation."

Silk Merchants Sell at a Loss: Chinese Silk Exports Surge; More Than 1,900 Bales Exported in the Second Half of March 99

The Industrial News Agency reports that although the price increase in the overseas silk market, New York, was minimal, silk merchants were mostly selling at a painful loss to cash in. Therefore, the export volume actually increased sharply. According to the data released yesterday by the Silk Group of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, raw silk exports in the second half of last month (March 16th to 31st) were 954 bales, and waste silk was 972 bales, totaling 1,926 bales. The breakdown is as follows:

Europe: 329 bales of white filature silk, 10 bales of Chefoo silk, 10 bales of grey silk, 15 bales of dupion silk, and 235 bales of waste silk, totaling 599 bales.

Americas: 375 bales of white filature silk, 10 bales of dupion silk, and 309 bales of waste silk, totaling 694 bales.

India: 37 bales of white tussah silk and 16 bales of dupion silk, totaling 53 bales.

Other countries: 25 bales of white filature silk, 26 bales of Chefoo silk, 23 bales of white tussah silk, 3 bales of yellow silk, 61 bales of yellow tussah silk, 14 bales of dupion silk, and 428 bales of waste silk, totaling 580 bales.

Total: 1,926 bales.

The Industry and Commerce Loan Association Continues to Approve Loans: A Total of 23,600 Yuan in Loans Approved for Fifty Businesses; Applicants Are Advised Not to Falsify Capital to Avoid Rejection 101

The Shanghai Industry and Commerce Loan Review Committee held its 26th meeting at 4:30 PM on the 1st of this month at the China National Products Bank on Tianjin Road. The committee members present were Cai Zengji, Song Ziliang, Wang Xiaolai, Bei Songsun, (Song Dai), Du Yuesheng, (Wang Dai), Chen Guangfu, (Cai Dai). The meeting was chaired by Cai Zengji.

After reporting on routine business, the committee considered 67 applications for small credit loans. After review, it was decided to approve one application, approve one for half the amount, and approve 48 with reduced amounts, totaling 23,600 yuan in loans. The remaining 17 applications were rejected because either the business did not comply with loan principles, or the intended use of the loan did not comply with regulations, or the applicants had declared a cessation of business.

The association will notify each applicant separately of the results. The association has also noted that applicants frequently fail to comply with the principle that the loan amount should not exceed half of the capital, and often falsely report their capital in the hopes of obtaining a loan. Therefore, at the 24th regular meeting, it was decided that all applications that do not comply with the regulations will be rejected without investigation. It has been observed that there are still many cases of falsely reported capital. The association is strictly enforcing the resolution and rejecting these applications for investigation. Therefore, it is hoped that factories wishing to apply for loans will pay close attention to this matter and inquire in detail when obtaining the application form from the association's office on the upper floor of the China National Products Bank on Tianjin Road, so as to avoid repeating the same mistakes and being rejected.

Ministry of Finance Approves: Acceptance Bills Must Be Stamped 109

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, requesting that commercial acceptance bills be encouraged for circulation and, following the example of checks, be exempted from stamp tax. Now, the Ministry of Finance has approved, opening with “Your telegram has been noted.” After investigating, the Ministry of Finance said that acceptance bills are documents for payment on a fixed date. Although their usage is different from ordinary drafts, they are still a type of draft by nature, which is already included in the scope of documents for money transfer. The Ministry of Finance said that stamp duty should be paid in accordance with the law. It also said that only the item of checks has been temporarily exempted this time in Article 16 and Tax Rate Table 4 of the amended Stamp Duty Law. As drafts are not on the list, there is no way to handle this following the example of checks. The Ministry of Finance said that what was requested should not be discussed. This is the response.
